## Callbacks

These functions are called by the engine automatically:

| Callback | Description |
|----------|-------------|
| `luna.load()` | Called once after the script is loaded |
| `luna.update(dt)` | Called every frame; `dt` is elapsed seconds |
| `luna.draw()` | Called every frame for rendering |
| `luna.keypressed(key)` | Called when a keyboard key is pressed |
| `luna.keyreleased(key)` | Called when a keyboard key is released |
| `luna.mousepressed(x, y, button)` | Called when a mouse button is pressed |
| `luna.mousereleased(x, y, button)` | Called when a mouse button is released |
| `luna.touchpressed(id, x, y, dx, dy, pressure)` | Called on touch start |
| `luna.touchmoved(id, x, y, dx, dy, pressure)` | Called on touch move |
| `luna.touchreleased(id, x, y, dx, dy, pressure)` | Called on touch end |
| `luna.resize(w, h)` | Called when window is resized |
| `luna.focus(focused)` | Called when window gains/loses focus |
| `luna.quit()` | Called when the window is closed |
| `luna.gamepadpressed(id, button)` | Called on gamepad button press |
| `luna.gamepadreleased(id, button)` | Called on gamepad button release |
| `luna.gamepadaxis(id, axis, value)` | Called on gamepad axis change |

### Functions

#### `luna.graphics.applyTransform()`

Applies the given Transform object to the current transform stack.

---

#### `luna.graphics.arc`

Draws a filled or outlined arc segment centered at (x, y) with the given radius.

**Parameters:**

- `mode` — Draw mode: 'fill' or 'line'.
- `x` — Center X coordinate in pixels.
- `y` — Center Y coordinate in pixels.
- `radius` — Arc radius in pixels.
- `angle1` — Start angle in radians.
- `angle2` — End angle in radians.
- `segments` — Optional number of line segments for smoothness.
Draws an arc.
Lua API: luna.graphics.arc(mode, x, y, radius, angle1, angle2, segments?)

*Source: [src/lua_api/graphics_api.rs](src/lua_api/graphics_api.rs#L1548)*

---

#### `luna.graphics.circle(mode, x, y, r)`

Draws a filled or outlined circle centered at (x, y) with the given radius.

**Parameters:**

- `mode` — Draw mode: 'fill' or 'line'.
- `x` — Center X coordinate in pixels.
- `y` — Center Y coordinate in pixels.
- `radius` — Circle radius in pixels.
- `segments` — Optional number of line segments (default auto).
Draws a circle.
Lua API: luna.graphics.circle(mode, x, y, r)

*Source: [src/lua_api/graphics_api.rs](src/lua_api/graphics_api.rs#L772)*

## luna.graphics_ext

Lua API bindings for Phase 24 graphics extension types.

Provides UserData wrappers and factory functions for extended graphics
subsystems: Light2D, TextureAtlas, DrawLayer, Viewport, ViewportScale,
SpriteSheet, PolygonMap, GraphRenderer, LargeMapRenderer, ColumnBatch,
Camera2D, Animation, Trail, DecalSurface, and PaletteLUT.

*157 entries | 0 documented*

## luna.window

*34 entries | 34 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.window.close()`

---

#### `luna.window.getDesktopDimensions()`

*Source: [src/lua_api/window_api.rs](src/lua_api/window_api.rs#L236)*

---

---

#### `mlua:cancelAll()`

Cancels and removes every pending timer entry from this scheduler.

Cancels a specific named timer that was scheduled on this scheduler.

---

#### `mlua:getCount()`

*Source: [src/lua_api/timer_api.rs](src/lua_api/timer_api.rs#L204)*

---

#### `mlua:getInterval(id)`

**Parameters:**

- `id` — Timer ID returned when the timer was created.

- `id` — Timer ID.

---

#### `mlua:getTimeScale()`

Returns the current time-scale factor applied to all timers in this scheduler.

**Returns:** Time scale as a number (1.0 = real time, 0.5 = half speed).

*Source: [src/lua_api/timer_api.rs](src/lua_api/timer_api.rs#L251)*

---

#### `mlua:isEmpty()`

Returns whether the scheduler has no active timer entries.

*Source: [src/lua_api/timer_api.rs](src/lua_api/timer_api.rs#L211)*

---

#### `mlua:isPaused(id)`

Returns whether the scheduler is currently paused and not advancing timers.

**Parameters:** `id`

**Returns:** true if paused, false if running.

*Source: [src/lua_api/timer_api.rs](src/lua_api/timer_api.rs#L157)*

---

#### `mlua:pause(id)`

Pauses the scheduler so no pending callbacks fire until resumed.

**Parameters:** `id`

*Source: [src/lua_api/timer_api.rs](src/lua_api/timer_api.rs#L146)*

---

#### `mlua:resetEvent(id)`

Resets the elapsed time of the given timer so it fires again after its full interval.

**Parameters:**

- `id` — Timer ID to reset.

*Source: [src/lua_api/timer_api.rs](src/lua_api/timer_api.rs#L230)*

---

#### `mlua:resume(id)`

**Parameters:** `id`

*Source: [src/lua_api/timer_api.rs](src/lua_api/timer_api.rs#L150)*

---

#### `mlua:setInterval(id, interval)`

Changes the repeat interval of an existing timer without recreating it.

**Parameters:**

- `id` — Timer ID.
- `interval` — New interval in seconds.

*Source: [src/lua_api/timer_api.rs](src/lua_api/timer_api.rs#L221)*

---

#### `mlua:setTimeScale(scale)`

Sets a time-scale factor that speeds up or slows down all timers in the scheduler.

**Parameters:**

- `scale` — Time multiplier (1.0 = real time, 2.0 = double speed).

*Source: [src/lua_api/timer_api.rs](src/lua_api/timer_api.rs#L241)*

---

#### `mlua:update(dt)`

---

#### `Transform:reset()`

---

#### `Transform:rotate(angle)`

---

#### `Transform:scale(sx, [sy])`

- `sx` — Horizontal scale factor.
- `sy` — Vertical scale factor (defaults to sx if omitted).

---

#### `Transform:shear(kx, ky)`

Applies a shear (skew) transformation to the internal matrix.

**Parameters:**

- `kx` — Horizontal shear factor.
- `ky` — Vertical shear factor.

*Source: [src/lua_api/math_api.rs](src/lua_api/math_api.rs#L123)*

---

#### `Transform:transformPoint(x, y)`

**Parameters:**

- `x` — Input X coordinate.
- `y` — Input Y coordinate.

**Returns:** Transformed x, y coordinates.

---

#### `Transform:translate(dx, dy)`

**Parameters:**

- `dx` — Horizontal offset in pixels.
- `dy` — Vertical offset in pixels.

*Source: [src/lua_api/math_api.rs](src/lua_api/math_api.rs#L93)*

#### `MidiPlayer:getTempoScale()`

## luna.physics

*94 entries | 94 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.physics.addDistanceJoint`

Adds a distance joint that maintains a fixed separation between two body anchor points.

**Parameters:**

- `world` — World ID.
- `body1` — First body ID.
- `body2` — Second body ID.
- `x1`, `y1` — Anchor on body1 in local coordinates.
- `x2`, `y2` — Anchor on body2 in local coordinates.

**Returns:** New joint ID.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L1442)*

---

#### `luna.physics.addFrictionJoint`

Adds a friction joint that resists relative movement and rotation between two bodies.

**Parameters:**

- `world` — World ID.
- `body1` — First body ID.
- `body2` — Second body ID.
- `ax`, `ay` — World-space anchor point.

**Returns:** New joint ID.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L1814)*

---

#### `luna.physics.addGearJoint(world_id_val, body_a, body_b, ax, ay)`

Adds a gear joint that couples two revolute or prismatic joints so they move in sync.

**Parameters:**

- `world` — World ID.
- `joint1` — First revolute or prismatic joint ID.
- `joint2` — Second revolute or prismatic joint ID.
- `ratio` — Gear ratio between the two joints.

**Returns:** New joint ID.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L1955)*

---

#### `luna.physics.addMotorJoint(world_id_val, body_a, body_b, cf)`

Adds a motor joint that drives one body toward a target position relative to another.

**Parameters:**

- `world` — World ID.
- `body1` — First body ID (reference).
- `body2` — Second body ID (driven).

**Returns:** New joint ID.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L1850)*

---

#### `luna.physics.addMouseJoint(world_id_val, body_id_val, tx, ty, mf)`

Adds a mouse joint that applies a spring force pulling a body toward a target point.

**Parameters:**

- `world` — World ID.
- `body` — Body ID to control.
- `x`, `y` — Initial target position in world coordinates.

**Returns:** New joint ID.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L1875)*

---

#### `luna.physics.addPrismaticJoint`

Adds a prismatic joint that constrains two bodies to slide along a single axis.

**Parameters:**

- `world` — World ID.
- `body1` — First body ID.
- `body2` — Second body ID.
- `ax`, `ay` — World-space anchor point.
- `axisX`, `axisY` — Slide axis direction (unit vector).

**Returns:** New joint ID.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L1480)*

---

#### `luna.physics.addPulleyJoint(world_id_val, body_a, body_b, ax, ay)`

Adds a pulley joint linking two bodies through a rope of fixed total length.

**Parameters:**

- `world` — World ID.
- `body1` — First body ID.
- `body2` — Second body ID.
- `gx1`, `gy1` — Ground anchor for body1 in world coordinates.
- `gx2`, `gy2` — Ground anchor for body2 in world coordinates.
- `ax1`, `ay1` — Body1 attachment point in local coordinates.
- `ax2`, `ay2` — Body2 attachment point in local coordinates.
- `ratio` — Pulley ratio (1.0 = symmetric).

**Returns:** New joint ID.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L1929)*

---

#### `luna.physics.addRevoluteJoint(world_id_val, body_a, body_b, ax, ay)`

Adds a revolute joint that constrains two bodies to rotate around a shared anchor point.

**Parameters:**

- `world` — World ID.
- `body1` — First body ID.
- `body2` — Second body ID.
- `ax`, `ay` — World-space anchor point to revolve around.

**Returns:** New joint ID.

---

#### `luna.physics.addRopeJoint`

**Parameters:**

- `world` — World ID.
- `body1` — First body ID.
- `body2` — Second body ID.
- `x1`, `y1` — Anchor on body1 in local coordinates.
- `x2`, `y2` — Anchor on body2 in local coordinates.
- `maxLength` — Maximum allowed distance in world units.

**Returns:** New joint ID.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L1545)*

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L248)*

---

#### `luna.filesystem.lines(path)`

Returns an iterator over lines in a text file.

**Parameters:** `path`

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L414)*

---

#### `luna.filesystem.openFile(path, mode_str)`

Opens a file and returns a readable/writable file handle.

**Parameters:** `path`, `mode_str`

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L209)*

---

#### `luna.filesystem.pollAsync(handle_id)`

Poll an async load handle. Returns status, data-or-nil.

Status is "pending", "done", or "error".

**Parameters:** `handle_id`

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L462)*

---

#### `luna.filesystem.read(path)`

Reads a text file and returns its contents as a string.

**Parameters:** `path`

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L140)*

---

#### `luna.filesystem.readAsync(path)`

Start loading a file in the background. Returns a numeric handle.

**Parameters:** `path`

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L440)*

---

#### `luna.filesystem.remove(path)`

Permanently deletes the file at the given path from the save directory.

**Parameters:**

- `path` — Relative path to the file to delete.

**Returns:** true on success, or nil plus an error string on failure.

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L292)*

---

#### `luna.filesystem.setIdentity(name)`

Sets the identity string that names the game's sandboxed save-data directory.

**Parameters:**

- `name` — Application identity string (e.g. 'mygame').

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L402)*

---

#### `luna.filesystem.write(path, data)`

Writes a string to a file, creating it if needed.

**Parameters:** `path`, `data`

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L158)*

---

### FileHandle Methods

#### `FileHandle:close()`

Flushes any pending writes and closes the file handle.

**Returns:** true on success, or nil plus an error string on failure.

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L105)*

---

#### `FileHandle:flush()`

Flushes all buffered writes to disk without closing the handle.

**Returns:** true on success, or nil plus an error string on failure.

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L94)*

---

#### `FileHandle:getMode()`

Returns the access mode the file was opened with.

**Returns:** One of 'r' (read), 'w' (write), or 'a' (append).

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L85)*

---

#### `FileHandle:getSize()`

Returns the size of the open file in bytes.

**Returns:** File size as an integer number of bytes.

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L76)*

---

#### `FileHandle:isEOF()`

Returns whether the read cursor has reached the end of the file.

**Returns:** true if at end-of-file, false otherwise.

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L116)*

---

#### `FileHandle:read(count)`

Reads a text file and returns its contents as a string.

**Parameters:** `count`

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L16)*

---

#### `FileHandle:readLine()`

Reads the next line of text from the file and returns it as a string.

**Returns:** The line string (without newline), or nil at end of file.

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L28)*

---

#### `FileHandle:seek(pos)`

Seeks the file position to the given byte offset from the start.

**Parameters:**

- `offset` — Byte position to seek to (0-based).

**Returns:** The new byte position, or nil plus an error string on failure.

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L52)*

---

#### `FileHandle:tell()`

Returns the current read/write byte offset from the start of the file.

**Returns:** Current byte offset as an integer.

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L64)*

---

#### `FileHandle:write(data)`

Writes a string to a file, creating it if needed.

**Parameters:** `data`

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L37)*

---


## luna.particle

Registers the `luna.particle.*` particle-system API.

Provides functions for creating, updating, drawing, and controlling
emitter-based particle effects from Lua game scripts.

*93 entries | 0 documented*

## luna.thread

Registers the `luna.thread` namespace.

Provides Lua-level multithreading: create background threads that run
independent Lua VMs and communicate via thread-safe channels.

*7 entries | 7 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.thread.getChannel(name)`

Get or create a named global channel (singleton, shared across threads).

**Parameters:** `name`

*Source: [src/lua_api/thread_api.rs](src/lua_api/thread_api.rs#L120)*

---

#### `luna.thread.newChannel()`

Create an unnamed thread-safe channel for inter-thread communication.

*Source: [src/lua_api/thread_api.rs](src/lua_api/thread_api.rs#L107)*

---

#### `luna.thread.newThread(code)`

Create a new background thread from a Lua code string.

The thread gets its own Lua VM and can communicate via channels.

**Parameters:** `code`

*Source: [src/lua_api/thread_api.rs](src/lua_api/thread_api.rs#L95)*

---

### ThreadHandle Methods

#### `ThreadHandle:getError()`

Returns the last error from the thread, or nil.

*Source: [src/lua_api/thread_api.rs](src/lua_api/thread_api.rs#L65)*

---

#### `ThreadHandle:isRunning()`

Returns whether the thread is currently executing.

*Source: [src/lua_api/thread_api.rs](src/lua_api/thread_api.rs#L59)*

---

#### `ThreadHandle:start(args)`

Starts a thread, passing optional arguments.

**Parameters:** `args`

*Source: [src/lua_api/thread_api.rs](src/lua_api/thread_api.rs#L38)*

---

#### `ThreadHandle:wait()`

Blocks the calling coroutine until the background thread finishes.

**Returns:** The thread's return value, or nil plus an error string on failure.

*Source: [src/lua_api/thread_api.rs](src/lua_api/thread_api.rs#L52)*

---


## luna.ai

Registers the `luna.ai.*` game AI toolkit API.

Provides factory functions and UserData wrappers for AI subsystems:
AIWorld, Agent, Blackboard, StateMachine, BehaviorTree, SteeringManager,
PathGrid, FlowField, QLearner, UtilityAI, GOAPPlanner, InfluenceMap,
Squad, and CommandQueue.

## luna.data

Registers the `luna.data.*` binary data, compression, hashing, and encoding API.

*8 entries | 8 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.data.compress(format_str, raw_data, [level])`

Compresses data using the given algorithm ('deflate', 'gzip', 'lz4').

**Parameters:** `format_str`, `raw_data`, `level`

*Source: [src/lua_api/data_api.rs](src/lua_api/data_api.rs#L43)*

---

#### `luna.data.decode(format_str, encoded)`

Decodes binary data from a buffer according to a pack-format string.

**Parameters:**

- `format` — Pack-format string (same syntax as string.pack).
- `data` — Binary string or ByteData buffer to read from.

**Returns:** Decoded Lua values followed by the next unread byte offset.

*Source: [src/lua_api/data_api.rs](src/lua_api/data_api.rs#L107)*

---

#### `luna.data.decompress(format_str, compressed_data)`

Decompresses data using the given algorithm.

**Parameters:** `format_str`, `compressed_data`

*Source: [src/lua_api/data_api.rs](src/lua_api/data_api.rs#L59)*

---

#### `luna.data.encode(format_str, raw_data)`

Encodes Lua values into a binary string using a pack-format string.

**Parameters:**

- `format` — Pack-format string (same syntax as string.pack).
- `...` — Values to encode.

**Returns:** Binary string containing the packed bytes.

*Source: [src/lua_api/data_api.rs](src/lua_api/data_api.rs#L89)*

---

#### `luna.data.encodeToml(table)`

Encodes a Lua table as a TOML string.

**Parameters:** `table`

*Source: [src/lua_api/data_api.rs](src/lua_api/data_api.rs#L129)*

---

#### `luna.data.hash(algo_str, raw_data)`

Returns the cryptographic hash (md5, sha1, sha256) of the input.

**Parameters:** `algo_str`, `raw_data`

*Source: [src/lua_api/data_api.rs](src/lua_api/data_api.rs#L72)*

---

#### `luna.data.newByteData(value)`

Creates a new mutable byte buffer of the given size.

**Parameters:** `value`

*Source: [src/lua_api/data_api.rs](src/lua_api/data_api.rs#L20)*

---

#### `luna.data.parseToml(input)`

Parses a TOML string and returns a Lua table.

**Parameters:** `input`

*Source: [src/lua_api/data_api.rs](src/lua_api/data_api.rs#L119)*

---

## luna.sound

Registers the `luna.sound.*` decoded audio sample manipulation API.

*4 entries | 4 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.sound.clearMidiSoundFont()`

Unloads the active SoundFont so the MIDI player falls back to built-in defaults.

*Source: [src/lua_api/sound_api.rs](src/lua_api/sound_api.rs#L136)*

---

#### `luna.sound.hasMidiSoundFont()`

Returns whether a SoundFont is currently loaded for the MIDI synthesizer.

**Returns:** true if a SoundFont is loaded, false otherwise.

*Source: [src/lua_api/sound_api.rs](src/lua_api/sound_api.rs#L125)*

---

#### `luna.sound.newSoundData(args)`

Creates a raw PCM audio buffer for building procedurally generated sound.

**Parameters:**

- `samples` — Total number of PCM samples to allocate.
- `sampleRate` — Sample rate in Hz (e.g. 44100).
- `bitDepth` — Bit depth per sample (8 or 16).
- `channels` — Number of channels (1 = mono, 2 = stereo).

**Returns:** New SoundData object ID.

*Source: [src/lua_api/sound_api.rs](src/lua_api/sound_api.rs#L35)*

---

#### `luna.sound.setMidiSoundFont(path)`

Sets the SoundFont (.sf2) file that the MIDI synthesizer uses for instrument samples.

**Parameters:**

- `path` — File path to the .sf2 SoundFont file.

*Source: [src/lua_api/sound_api.rs](src/lua_api/sound_api.rs#L101)*

---


## luna.graph

Registers the `luna.graph.*` directed-graph and item-flow simulation API.

Exposes `LuaGraph`, `LuaNode`, `LuaEdge`, and `LuaGraphItem` UserData types
wrapping `crate::graph::Graph` with callback dispatch for simulation events.

## luna.tilemap

Registers the `luna.tilemap.*` tile map, tileset, autotile, and procedural generation API.

Exposes `LuaTileSet`, `LuaTileMap`, `LuaAutoTileSheet`, `LuaMapBlock`, `LuaMapGroup`,
`LuaMapScript`, and `LuaMapGen` UserData types wrapping the `crate::tilemap` module.

All Lua-facing tile/layer/segment indices are **1-based**; Rust internals are 0-based.

*137 entries | 137 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.tilemap.fromScreenHex(sx, sy, size)`

luna.tilemap.fromScreenHex(sx, sy, size)

**Parameters:** `sx`, `sy`, `size`

*Source: [src/lua_api/tilemap_api.rs](src/lua_api/tilemap_api.rs#L2235)*

*Source: [src/lua_api/tilemap_api.rs](src/lua_api/tilemap_api.rs#L2197)*

---

#### `luna.tilemap.hexArea(q, r, radius)`

Returns all hex cell coordinates within a given radius of center (q, r).

**Parameters:**

- `q` — Center q coordinate.
- `r` — Center r coordinate.
- `radius` — Radius in hex steps (1 = immediate ring, 2 = two rings, etc.).

**Returns:** Table of {q, r} coordinates for every cell within the radius.

*Source: [src/lua_api/tilemap_api.rs](src/lua_api/tilemap_api.rs#L2355)*

---

## luna.debug

Registers the `luna.devtools.*` runtime diagnostics and developer tools API.

Five subsystems: structured logger, hierarchical profiler, frame statistics,
file watcher, and Lua debug bridge. All module-level functions — no
registered types.

*33 entries | 33 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.debug.clearLog()`

Clears all log history.

*Source: [src/lua_api/debug_api.rs](src/lua_api/debug_api.rs#L283)*

---

#### `luna.debug.clearWatches()`

Clears all watched paths.

*Source: [src/lua_api/debug_api.rs](src/lua_api/debug_api.rs#L614)*

---

#### `luna.debug.eval(code)`

Evaluates a Lua string and returns success flag plus results.

**Parameters:** `code`

*Source: [src/lua_api/debug_api.rs](src/lua_api/debug_api.rs#L653)*

---

#### `luna.debug.getCallStack(max_depth)`

Returns the Lua call stack as a table of stack frames.

Uses Lua's debug.getinfo to walk the stack.

**Parameters:** `max_depth`

*Source: [src/lua_api/debug_api.rs](src/lua_api/debug_api.rs#L626)*

---

#### `luna.debug.getFrameHistory()`

Returns the raw frame time history.

*Source: [src/lua_api/debug_api.rs](src/lua_api/debug_api.rs#L492)*

---

## luna.debugbridge

Registers the `luna.debugbridge.*` TCP debug server API.

Embeds a JSON-over-TCP server (127.0.0.1 only) inside the running game.
External tools (VS Code extension, MCP server) connect to inspect and
control the game at runtime. Network I/O runs on a background thread;
Lua-dependent methods are queued and dispatched via `poll()` on the main thread.

*15 entries | 15 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.debugbridge.broadcast(event, json_data)`

Broadcasts a JSON event to all connected clients.

**Parameters:** `event`, `json_data`

*Source: [src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs](src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs#L757)*

---

#### `luna.debugbridge.capturePrint(msg, [source], [line])`

Captures a print message and broadcasts it to connected clients.

**Parameters:** `msg`, `source`, `line`

*Source: [src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs](src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs#L608)*

---

#### `luna.debugbridge.clearPrintHistory()`

Clears the print history.

*Source: [src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs](src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs#L659)*

---

#### `luna.debugbridge.getClientCount()`

Returns the number of connected TCP clients.

*Source: [src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs](src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs#L438)*

---

#### `luna.debugbridge.getPerformance()`

Returns performance statistics.

*Source: [src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs](src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs#L706)*

---

#### `luna.debugbridge.getPort()`

Returns the server port (0 if not running).

*Source: [src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs](src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs#L429)*

---

#### `luna.debugbridge.getPrintHistory(count)`

Returns the print history.

**Parameters:** `count`

*Source: [src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs](src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs#L631)*

---

#### `luna.debugbridge.isRunning()`

Returns whether the server is currently running.

*Source: [src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs](src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs#L422)*

---

#### `luna.debugbridge.isScreenshotRequested()`

Returns whether a screenshot is currently requested.

*Source: [src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs](src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs#L743)*

---

#### `luna.debugbridge.poll()`

Poll for pending Lua-dependent requests from TCP clients.

Must be called each frame from luna.update().

*Source: [src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs](src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs#L448)*

---

#### `luna.debugbridge.recordFrame(dt)`

Records a frame time sample.

**Parameters:** `dt`

*Source: [src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs](src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs#L690)*

---

#### `luna.debugbridge.requestScreenshot(scale)`

Flags a screenshot request for the next frame.

**Parameters:** `scale`

## luna.docs

Registers the `luna.docs.*` documentation management API.

Provides engine-integrated documentation management: scanning runtime bindings,
loading TOML doc catalogs, validating completeness, computing quality metrics,
and exporting structured data for VS Code extension IntelliSense.

## luna.log

Structured game-level logging API (`luna.log.*`).

Exposes convenience logging functions so Lua scripts can emit messages at
specific severity levels and query or change the active log level at
runtime without going through the `luna.system` namespace.

*7 entries | 7 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.log.debug(message)`

Emit a debug-severity log message from Lua.

**Parameters:**

- `message` — The message string to log.

*Source: [src/lua_api/log_api.rs](src/lua_api/log_api.rs#L23)*

---

#### `luna.log.error(message)`

Emit an error-severity log message from Lua.

**Parameters:**

- `message` — The message string to log.

*Source: [src/lua_api/log_api.rs](src/lua_api/log_api.rs#L62)*

---

#### `luna.log.getLevel()`

Return the name of the currently active minimum log level.

**Returns:** One of `"off"`, `"error"`, `"warn"`, `"info"`, `"debug"`, `"trace"`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/log_api.rs](src/lua_api/log_api.rs#L113)*

---

#### `luna.log.info(message)`

Emit an info-severity log message from Lua.

**Parameters:**

- `message` — The message string to log.

*Source: [src/lua_api/log_api.rs](src/lua_api/log_api.rs#L36)*

---

#### `luna.log.print(level, message)`

Emit a log message from Lua at the specified severity level.

Accepts the same level strings as `luna.log.setLevel`: `"debug"`, `"info"`, `"warn"`, `"error"`, `"trace"`. Unknown levels fall back to `info`.

**Parameters:**

- `level` — Severity level string.
- `message` — The message string to log.

*Source: [src/lua_api/log_api.rs](src/lua_api/log_api.rs#L80)*

---

#### `luna.log.setLevel(level)`

Set the minimum severity level for runtime log messages.

**Parameters:**

- `level` — One of `"off"`, `"error"`, `"warn"`, `"info"`, `"debug"`, `"trace"`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/log_api.rs](src/lua_api/log_api.rs#L100)*

---

#### `luna.log.warn(message)`

Emit a warn-severity log message from Lua.

**Parameters:**

- `message` — The message string to log.

*Source: [src/lua_api/log_api.rs](src/lua_api/log_api.rs#L49)*

---

## luna.pathfinding

Registers the `luna.pathfinding.*` grid-based pathfinding API.

Exposes `NavGrid`, `UnitPathfinder`, and `FlowField` as Lua UserData
with 1-based tile coordinates at the Lua boundary.

## luna.patterns

Registers the `luna.patterns.*` software design patterns API.

Provides factory functions and UserData wrappers for reusable patterns:
EventBus (prioritized pub-sub), ObjectPool (object reuse), CommandStack
(undo/redo), ServiceLocator (DI container), Factory (named constructors),
and SimpleState (finite state machine).

*47 entries | 0 documented*

## luna.scene

Registers the `luna.scene.*` scene stack, registry, data store, and depth-sorter API.

The scene stack manages a LIFO stack of Lua scene tables with optional
visual transitions. Scene tables are stored via `mlua::RegistryKey` and
identified by `SceneId`. Inter-scene data is stored similarly.

The `DepthSorter` UserData batches draw callbacks by depth for ordered
compositing each frame.

*28 entries | 6 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.scene.clear()`

*(undocumented)*

*Source: [src/lua_api/scene_api.rs](src/lua_api/scene_api.rs#L305)*

---

### DepthSorter Methods

#### `DepthSorter:add(callback, depth)`

Registers a draw callback with a numeric depth for sorted rendering order.

**Parameters:**

- `callback` — Function to call when this entry is flushed.
- `depth` — Numeric depth; lower values are drawn first.

*Source: [src/lua_api/scene_api.rs](src/lua_api/scene_api.rs#L64)*

---

#### `DepthSorter:addObject(obj)`

Registers a drawable object (with a :draw() method) at the given depth.

**Parameters:**

- `obj` — Object implementing a :draw() method.
- `depth` — Numeric depth value for sort ordering.

*Source: [src/lua_api/scene_api.rs](src/lua_api/scene_api.rs#L78)*

---

#### `DepthSorter:clear()`

Removes all registered callbacks and objects from the depth sorter queue.

*Source: [src/lua_api/scene_api.rs](src/lua_api/scene_api.rs#L128)*

---

#### `DepthSorter:flush()`

Calls all queued draw callbacks in ascending depth order, then clears the queue.

*Source: [src/lua_api/scene_api.rs](src/lua_api/scene_api.rs#L95)*

---

#### `DepthSorter:getCount()`

Returns the number of callbacks and objects currently queued for rendering.

**Returns:** Queue length as an integer.

*Source: [src/lua_api/scene_api.rs](src/lua_api/scene_api.rs#L138)*

---

#### `DepthSorter:sort()`

Sorts the queued draw entries by depth value without flushing them.

*Source: [src/lua_api/scene_api.rs](src/lua_api/scene_api.rs#L89)*

---
